	<div class="entry-content-wrap">
		<header class="entry-header post-title title-align-center title-tablet-align-inherit title-mobile-align-inherit">
	<nav id="kadence-breadcrumbs" aria-label="Breadcrumbs"  class="kadence-breadcrumbs"><div class="kadence-breadcrumb-container"><span><a href="https://avirtuouswoman.org/" title="Home" itemprop="url" class="kadence-bc-home kadence-bc-home-icon" ><span><span class="kadence-svg-iconset svg-baseline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="kadence-svg-icon kadence-home-svg" fill="currentColor" version="1.1" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><title>Home</title><path d="M9.984 20.016h-4.969v-8.016h-3l9.984-9 9.984 9h-3v8.016h-4.969v-6h-4.031v6z"></path>
				</svg></span></span></a></span> <span class="bc-delimiter">/</span> <span><a href="https://avirtuouswoman.org/avirtuous-woman/" itemprop="url" ><span>A Virtuous Woman</span></a></span> <span class="bc-delimiter">/</span> <span class="kadence-bread-current">46 Delicious Summer Salads: Perfect for Picnics | What&#8217;s Your Favorite?</span></div></nav><h1 class="entry-title">46 Delicious Summer Salads: Perfect for Picnics | What&#8217;s Your Favorite?</h1></header><!-- .entry-header -->

<div class="entry-content single-content">
	
<p>There&#8217;s just something about the warm weather that always draws me outside. I love taking my family on picnics and during the warm weather months, we often eat outside at least once a week. Today I&#8217;m sharing a collection of <strong>summer salads perfect for picnics</strong>. Finding <a href="https://avirtuouswoman.org/how-to-plan-a-picnic/">the perfect picnic</a> recipes is an important part of the experience!</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img decoding="async" width="683" height="1024" src="https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/46-Summer-Salads-Perfect-for-Picnics-683x1024.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-92689" srcset="https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/46-Summer-Salads-Perfect-for-Picnics-683x1024.jpg 683w, https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/46-Summer-Salads-Perfect-for-Picnics-534x800.jpg 534w, https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/46-Summer-Salads-Perfect-for-Picnics-150x225.jpg 150w, https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/46-Summer-Salads-Perfect-for-Picnics.jpg 735w" sizes="(max-width: 683px) 100vw, 683px" /></figure></div>


<pre class="wp-block-preformatted"><em>Originally written: July 2020. Updated June 2024.</em></pre>



<p>Our family loves to enjoy the outdoors all year round. In the summer time, it&#8217;s so much fun to spend the day at a park and enjoy a picnic together. </p>



<p>A couple weeks ago we took Marlowe out to our county&#8217;s lake. It&#8217;s not real big and it&#8217;s often very quiet. Kind of like a secret treasure in the mountains. After our meal, Hannah and I decided to show Marlowe the water. I&#8217;d like for her to love playing with us in the lake!  Marlowe is about 20 weeks old now &#8211; so she was 18 weeks when we took her for the first time. </p>



<div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-9d6595d7 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">

<p>She wasn&#8217;t too sure about the water! Hopefully as we take her more often, she&#8217;ll start to enjoy it! </p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="768" src="https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/IMG_0122-1024x768.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-92637" srcset="https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/IMG_0122-1024x768.jpg 1024w, https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/IMG_0122-800x600.jpg 800w, https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/IMG_0122-1536x1152.jpg 1536w, https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/IMG_0122-2048x1536.jpg 2048w, https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/IMG_0122-550x413.jpg 550w, https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/IMG_0122-350x263.jpg 350w, https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/IMG_0122-260x195.jpg 260w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></figure>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="768" src="https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/IMG_0121-1024x768.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-92638" srcset="https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/IMG_0121-1024x768.jpg 1024w, https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/IMG_0121-800x600.jpg 800w, https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/IMG_0121-1536x1152.jpg 1536w, https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/IMG_0121-2048x1536.jpg 2048w, https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/IMG_0121-550x413.jpg 550w, https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/IMG_0121-350x263.jpg 350w, https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/IMG_0121-260x195.jpg 260w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></figure>



<p>We had several of our extended family members come out to the picnic and we enjoyed a very simple picnic meal. Really nothing fancy. Just some of our favorite sandwiches, this <a href="https://avirtuouswoman.org/easy-lunch-box-macaroni-pea-salad-with-cheese/">macaroni and pea salad</a>, and fruit snacks. But it was filling and tasted good and the kids had fun! </p>



<p>Picnics can be as simple as you like, but having some great picnic recipes and family favorites definitely makes it more fun and memorable!</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="768" src="https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/IMG_0124-1024x768.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-92639" srcset="https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/IMG_0124-1024x768.jpg 1024w, https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/IMG_0124-800x600.jpg 800w, https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/IMG_0124-1536x1152.jpg 1536w, https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/IMG_0124-2048x1536.jpg 2048w, https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/IMG_0124-550x413.jpg 550w, https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/IMG_0124-350x263.jpg 350w, https://avirtuouswoman.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/IMG_0124-260x195.jpg 260w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></figure>



<p>In our household, we’re vegetarian. In fact the large majority of our extended family is vegetarian as well. Sometimes I make vegetarian dinners that are just you know, naturally vegetarian. However, sometimes I take recipes that call for meat and replace the meat with a vegetarian option.</p>



<p>Being a&nbsp;<a href="https://avirtuouswoman.org/creation-diet-day-39/">vegetarian has many health benefits</a>.</p>



<p><strong>Vegetarian substitutions for meat:</strong></p>



<p>You’ll find these products in the freezer aisle or health food section of your local grocery store. You can also find these products at most health food stores like Whole Foods.</p>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>ground beef or turkey > <a href="https://www.morningstarfarms.com/en_US/products/meal-starters/morningstar-farms-meal-starters-grillers-recipe-crumbles-product.html" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">vegetarian burger crumbles</a></li>



<li>chicken > <a href="https://www.quorn.us/products/quorn-meatless-chicken-pieces" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Quorn Meatless Pieces</a></li>



<li>chicken breast > <a href="https://www.quorn.us/products/quorn-meatless-chicken-fillets" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Quorn Meatless Filets</a></li>



<li>shredded chicken or pork > <a href="https://amzn.to/2MOUcZ8" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">canned jackfruit</a></li>



<li>beef, chicken, or pork > black beans, pinto beans, or chickpeas</li>



<li>deli meats > <a href="https://lightlife.com/our-food/?active_filter=deli" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Lightlife Deli Slices</a></li>



<li>sausage > <a href="https://lightlife.com/product/gimme-lean-sausage/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Gimme Lean Breakfast Sausage</a>, <a href="https://fieldroast.com/products/field-roast/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Field Roast Apple Sage Sausage</a></li>



<li>tuna > chickpeas</li>



<li>bacon > <a aria-label="undefined (opens in a new tab)" href="https://www.morningstarfarms.com/en_US/products/breakfast/morningstar-farms-veggie-bacon-strips-product.html" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Morning Star Farms Veggie Bacon</a></li>



<li>pepperoni > <a aria-label="undefined (opens in a new tab)" href="http://yvesveggie.com/en/products/deli-slices/pepperoni/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Veggie Pepperoni</a></li>
</ul>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading">46 Summer Salads Perfect for Picnics</h2>



<p>I&#8217;m excited to share this collection of summer salads for you to look through and try. If you find a picnic recipe you love, be sure to leave and comment and let me know! </p>

<h3 class="kt-adv-headingb2e13a-fb wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-headingb2e13a-fb">Hi!  I'm Melissa!</h3>



<p>I’m Melissa, the heart and hands behind this community. My journey as a homemaker began over 33 years ago. I’m a wife and mom to five, stepmom to four, and Grandarling to 17 and counting! I love serving my family and making our house a space that feels like home to everyone who enters.</p>



<p><a href="https://homemakerssociety.com/about/"></a></p>
